    	}
    }

    	local v1 = p1 + Unit * (p3 - p1):Dot(Unit)

    local function snap_number_to_grid(p1, p2) --[[ snap_number_to_grid | Line: 50 ]]
    	local v1 = p1 % p2

  format_value (ModuleScript)
    Path: game.ReplicatedStorage.client.gui.insitux.widget.util.format_value
    --- DECOMPILED CODE ---
    local function v1(p1) --[[ format_value | Line: 2 | Upvalues: v1 (copy) ]]
    	if typeof(p1) == "Instance" then
    		return p1:GetFullName()
    	elseif type(p1) == "number" then
    		return string.format("%.4f", p1)
    	elseif type(p1) == "string" then
    		return ("\"%*\""):format(p1)
    	elseif type(p1) == "boolean" then
    		return tostring(p1)
    	elseif typeof(p1) == "Vector3" then
    		return string.format("(%.1f, %.1f, %.1f)", p1.X, p1.Y, p1.Z)
    	elseif typeof(p1) == "CFrame" then
    		return string.format("CFrame(%.1f, %.1f, %.1f)", p1.X, p1.Y, p1.Z)
    	elseif type(p1) == "table" then
    		local t = {}
    		for k, v in pairs(p1) do
    			table.insert(t, (("%*: %*"):format(tostring(k), (v1(v)))))
    		return ("{ %* }"):format((table.concat(t, ", ")))
    		return tostring(p1)
    return {
    	format_value = v1
    }
    --- END CODE ---
